     </section>
     <h2>
      Yamaha Mio Fazzio 2024
     </h2>
     <div class="read-more-less m-lg-b">
      <p class="info height-hidden">
       The Yamaha Mio Fazzio 2024 price in the Philippines starts from ₱92,900 . it is available in 3 colors, 1 variants in the Philippines. The Mio Fazzio is powered by a 125 cc engine, and has a Variable Speed gearbox. The Yamaha Mio Fazzio has a seating height of 750 mm and kerb weight of 95 kg. The Mio Fazzio comes with Disc front brakes and Drum rear brakes. Over 11 users have reviewed Mio Fazzio on basis of Features, Mileage, seating comfort, and engine performance. Mio Fazzio top competitors are Genio, Like 125 Italia, Mio Gear and Mio i 125.
      </p>
      <span class="js-read-more read-more" data-gtm="tracking" data-gtm-action="atf_content_read_more" data-gtm-category="atf" data-gtm-component="YamahaMio Fazzio.ModelPage.overviewTab" data-gtm-event="Widget_Tracking" data-gtm-label="" data-gtm-section="atf">

     <section class="shadow-dark m-lg-t p-lg">
      <h2>
       Recent Updates of Mio Fazzio
      </h2>
      <div class="read-more-less">
       <div class="info height-hidden dynamic-content content-hidden">
        <p>
         <h2>
          <strong>
           How many variants are there in the Yamaha Mio Fazzio?
          </strong>
         </h2>
         <p>
          <span>
           The Yamaha Mio Fazzio is a neo-retro-themed scooter, which shares its mechanical underpinnings with other 125cc scooters from the Japanese manufacturer. The Yamaha Mio Fazzio is being offered in a fully loaded variant, with all the features as standard.
          </span>
         </p>
         <h2>
          <strong>
           How much is the price of the Yamaha Mio Fazzio in the Philippines?
          </strong>
         </h2>
         <p>
          <span>
           The Yamaha Mio Fazzio is being offered in three colour options for the single variant on sale. The prices for the Mio Fazzio start at PHP 92,900 for the two colour options – Pastel Blue and Ivory White and go up to PHP 93,900 for the more-premium Matte Orange colour.
          </span>
         </p>
         <h2>
          <strong>
           Which is the most value-for-money variant of the Yamaha Mio Fazzio?
          </strong>
         </h2>
         <p>
          <span>
           The Yamaha Mio Fazzio is being offered in a single variant, and based on the prices at which it is on sale, it is worth buying. The main USP of the Yamaha Mio Fazzio is undoubtedly its overall design language, with the distinctive neo-retro looks giving it a unique proposition in the 125cc segment which is crowded by sporty-looking offerings with sharp-looking body panels. The curvaceous design language of the Yamaha Mio Fazzio makes it look different from other 125cc scooters.
          </span>
         </p>
         <h2>
          <strong>
           What features does the Yamaha Mio Fazzio get?
          </strong>
         </h2>
         <p>
          <span>
           The Yamaha Mio Fazzio has a neo-retro design language, which is characterised by a vertically-aligned rounded rectangular theme for the headlamp mounted on the handlebar cowl, clear lens turn indicators mounted on the front apron and tail section, tail lamp and the instrument console. The headlamp and tail lamp of the Yamaha Mio Fazzio are all LED units, with the former also getting daytime running LEDs.
          </span>
         </p>
         <p>
          <span>
           The front apron of the Yamaha Mio Fazzio has a matte black garnish part running from top to bottom. Meanwhile, the side body panels also have curvaceous designs, with rounded rectangular garnish bits towards the rear. The Yamaha Mio Fazzio has a black-themed engine and 12-inch alloy wheels, with silver-finished aluminium footrests for the pillion rider adding a nice contrast to the appearance of the scooter.
          </span>
         </p>
         <p>
          <span>
           Besides having a lid pocket and a compact bottle holder integrated into the back portion of the front apron, the Yamaha Mio Fazzio also has a 17.8-litre under-seat storage compartment. The vertically-aligned full-LCD instrument console of this neo-retro-themed scooter has a speedometer, odometer, and fuel gauge. Besides these features, the Yamaha Mio Fazzio also has a USB charging port within the lid pocket and two luggage hooks.
          </span>
         </p>
         <h2>
          <strong>
           How spacious is it?
          </strong>
         </h2>
         <p>
          <span>
           With a length of 1,820 mm, a width of 685 mm, and a height of 1,125 mm, the Yamaha Mio Fazzio is a compact-sized scooter that might not feel roomy enough for a taller rider. The floorboard of the scooter also feels compact, though the scooter has a decently-sized under-seat storage compartment, besides having two usable small storage spaces integrated into its front apron. The fuel tank of the Yamaha Mio Fazzio also measures 5.1 litres, which is decent for its size.
          </span>
         </p>
         <h2>
          <strong>
           What engine and transmission options are available?
          </strong>
         </h2>
         <p>
          <span>
           Powering the Yamaha Mio Fazzio is a tried-and-tested four-stroke, single-cylinder, air-cooled, 125cc engine, which also powers other Yamaha offerings in the 125cc scooter segment. Paired with a conventional belt-driven transmission, this engine delivers a maximum power output of 8.4 PS and a maximum torque output of 9.9 Nm.
          </span>
         </p>
         <h2>
          <strong>
           What’s the mileage of the Yamaha Mio Fazzio?
          </strong>
         </h2>
         <p>
          <span>
           Yamaha hasn’t reported the official fuel efficiency figure of the Mio Fazzio. However, the users of this neo-retro-themed scooter from Yamaha have claimed to achieve mileage of 45-48 km in their usual daily rides.
          </span>
         </p>
         <h2>
          <strong>
           How safe is the Yamaha Mio Fazzio?
          </strong>
         </h2>
         <p>
          <span>
           The Yamaha Mio Fazzio might not be a feature-rich scooter when it comes to safety, for it lacks many essentials like ABS or even a combined braking system. However, this scooter has a lockable under-seat storage compartment to keep your daily items safe and locked. It also comes with a disc brake at the front for a safe braking experience while riding.
          </span>
         </p>
         <h2>
          <strong>
           How many colour options are there?
          </strong>
         </h2>
         <p>
          <span>
           There are three colour options in the lineup of Yamaha Mio Fazzio for the Philippines two-wheeler market. These colour options include Pastel Blue, Ivory White, and Matte Orange. Among all the three colour choices on sale for the Yamaha Mio Fazzio, the Pastel Blue and Ivory White cost the same, with Matte Orange carrying a small premium over these two.
          </span>
         </p>
         <h2>
          <strong>
           Should you buy the 2024 Yamaha Mio Fazzio?
          </strong>
         </h2>
         <p>
          <span>
           For those who value style and design the most, the Yamaha Mio Fazzio comes across as a very desirable scooter. The chic styling and compact dimensions make the Mio Fazzio look distinctive in the 125cc scooter segment, with the vibrant colour options only adding to its eye-catchiness. As with every other Yamaha product, the engine feels refined and smooth, with the scooter also being light and agile to ride, thanks to its compact dimensions and a light kerb weight of just 95 kg.
          </span>
         </p>
         <h2>
          <strong>
           What are my alternatives?
          </strong>
         </h2>
         <p>
          <span>
           Besides its stablemates in the 125cc category like the Mio Gear and Mio i 125, the Yamaha Mio Fazzio also competes with other sportier-looking 125cc scooters like Honda Click 125 and Suzuki Burgman Street. Besides these two direct rivals from traditional Japanese brands, the Yamaha Mio Fazzio is also a potent alternative to other scooters like Kymco Super Z 150, Skygo Blink 125, Keeway SIP 125, and Benelli VZ 125i.
          </span>
         </p>
         <h2>
          <strong>
           Other things to consider
          </strong>
         </h2>
         <p>
          <span>
           The Yamaha Mio Fazzio is purely for those who prefer form over functionality. While the scooter is decently practical for its size and price, it misses out on several other features and feels a bit basic in a couple of parameters. The smaller size of the scooter is another concern for taller riders, who might not find the floorboard too spacious. For those who want a more comfortable and practical scooter, they should look for other alternatives in the 125cc segment.
          </span>
         </p>
         <p>
         </p>
        </p>
        <h3>
         Yamaha Mio Fazzio Price
        </h3>
        <p>
         The Mio Fazzio is priced at ₱92,900 .
        </p>
        <h3>
         Yamaha Mio Fazzio Variants
        </h3>
        <p>
         There are 1 variants available of Mio Fazzio: Standard.
        </p>
        <h3>
         Yamaha Mio Fazzio Power-trains
        </h3>
        <p>
         The Mio Fazzio is powered by a Air Cooled Fuel Injection 125 cc 1 Cylinder engine that gives 8.3hp of power at 6500 rpm and 9.9 Nm Torque at 5000 rpm. It comes with the option of a Variable Speed transmission gearbox. The Mio Fazzio has a seat height of 750 mm. The Front Tyre size is 110/70 R12 &amp; Rear Tyre size is 110/70 R12.
        </p>
        <h3>
         Yamaha Mio Fazzio Features
        </h3>
        <p>
         Features Chassis, Suspension &amp; Brake include Telescopic Fork Front Suspension, Unit Swing Rear Suspension, Disc Front Brake, Drum Rear Brake, Underbone Body Frame Type and Dual Stepped Seat Type.
         <br/>
         Features for Console include Digital Odometer, Digital Fuel Gauge, Display Screen and Digital Speedometer.
        </p>
        <h3>
         Yamaha Mio Fazzio Competitors
        </h3>
        <p>
         The Mio Fazzio Competitors are:
         <a class="theme-link text-accent" href="https://www.zigwheels.ph/new-motorcycles/honda/genio" title="Honda Genio">

         </a>
         ,
         <a class="theme-link text-accent" href="https://www.zigwheels.ph/new-motorcycles/kymco/like-125" title="Kymco Like 125 Italia">
          Kymco Like 125 Italia
         </a>
         ,
         <a class="theme-link text-accent" href="https://www.zigwheels.ph/new-motorcycles/yamaha/mio-gear" title="Yamaha Mio Gear">
          Yamaha Mio Gear
         </a>
         and
         <a class="theme-link text-accent" href="https://www.zigwheels.ph/new-motorcycles/yamaha/mio-i-125" title="Yamaha Mio i 125">
          Yamaha Mio i 125
         </a>
         .
        </p>

     <section class="shadow-dark p-lg expert-review info dynamic-content">
      <h2>
       Yamaha Mio Fazzio Review 2024
      </h2>
      <div class="m-sm-b m-md-t">
       <h3>
        <strong class="f-bold">
         <a href="https://www.zigwheels.ph/authors/abhishek-katariya ">
          Abhishek Katariya
         </a>
         says
        </strong>
       </h3>
       <span class="author-img">
        <img alt="Abhishek Katariya" class="lazy" data-src="https://imgcdnblog.carbay.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/07/29061750/WhatsApp-Image-2020-02-12-at-16.21.19.jpeg" height="50" src="https://www.zigwheels.ph/2021/images/1x1.png" title="Abhishek Katariya" width="50"/>
       </span>
      </div>
      <div class="read-more-less">
       <div class="height-hidden dynamic-content content-hidden">
        <p>
         <span>
          Yamaha Mio Fazzio is a new member of the Mio scooter range. It has a seat height of 750mm, a wheelbase of 1,280mm, and 135 mm minimum ground clearance. The scooter is available in three colors in the Phillippines- white, blue, and red. It has an urban, modern appeal and stands out from the other entry-level scooters with impressive technology and premium features. With Mio Fazzio, Yamaha wants to change the misconception that scooters are soulless machines. The scooter offers an enjoyable and thrilling experience on two wheels. The starting price of the scooter is ₱88,900.
         </span>
        </p>
       </div>
       <span class="js-read-more read-more">
        Read More
       </span>
       <span class="js-read-less read-less content-read-less scroll-to-parent-pos hide">

       </span>

      <div class="accordion-list m-lg-t">
       <div class="accordion border-top">
        <h3 class="acc-title scroll-to-parent-pos" onclick="gd.common.pushDataLayers('YamahaMio Fazzio.ModelPage.overviewTab', '', 'click_section', 'Widget_Tracking', 'expert_review','2');">
         Yamaha Mio Fazzio Design
        </h3>
        <div class="acc-panel">
         <p>
          <span>
           The Yamaha Mio Fazzio is an elegant and sophisticated scooter with fresh styling and modern design. It is one of the most charming additions to the Mio scooter range.  It effortlessly combines a touch of modern minimalism with an infusion of retro-inspired design. The scooter has been designed keeping in mind the young generation and people who are always on the go due to their busy lifestyles. Its minimalist and sleek lines create a sense of refinement and elegance, while the funky and funky color schemes give a playful touch to this scooter.
          </span>
         </p>
         <p>
          <span>
           The white color of this scooter makes it look like a Tic-Tac on wheels. On the bodywork, it has contrasting cyan accents, giving it a distinct Yamaha flair. It boasts a round headlamp and oval signal lamps up front. The retro oval styling has been carried over to all the lights at the rear and the side. These eye-catching details represent Yamaha’s unwavering dedication to combining innovation and style. Despite its lightweight design, it is very durable and reliable.
          </span>
         </p>
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="accordion border-top">
        <h3 class="acc-title scroll-to-parent-pos" onclick="gd.common.pushDataLayers('YamahaMio Fazzio.ModelPage.overviewTab', '', 'click_section', 'Widget_Tracking', 'expert_review','3');">
         Mio Fazzio Ride &amp; Handling
        </h3>
        <div class="acc-panel">
         <p>
          <span>
           The Yamaha Mio Fazzio is automatic and easy to maneuver, even by beginners. Due to its lightweight frame, you will find it easy to move around congested roads and traffic. You don’t need to have plenty of knowledge about two-wheelers to operate this scooter. The stop-and-start system automatically turns the engine off automatically at full stops, improving fuel consumption.
          </span>
         </p>
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="accordion border-top">
        <h3 class="acc-title scroll-to-parent-pos" onclick="gd.common.pushDataLayers('YamahaMio Fazzio.ModelPage.overviewTab', '', 'click_section', 'Widget_Tracking', 'expert_review','4');">
         Yamaha Mio Fazzio Engine &amp; Fuel Consumption
        </h3>
        <div class="acc-panel">
         <p>
          <span>
           The Yamaha Mio Fazzio is powered by a 125 cc 1-cylinder engine with fuel injection and air cooling. The engine is equipped with a small motor generator, allowing a quiet engine start. It produces an impressive 8.3 horsepower at 6500 rpm and 9.9 Nm of torque at 5000 rpm. You also get a variable-speed transmission gearbox option with the scooter. It is available in V-belt automatic transmission. The hydraulic single-disc front brake provides superior stopping power. The fuel tank easily holds up to 5 liters of gas.
          </span>
         </p>
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="accordion border-top">
        <h3 class="acc-title scroll-to-parent-pos" onclick="gd.common.pushDataLayers('YamahaMio Fazzio.ModelPage.overviewTab', '', 'click_section', 'Widget_Tracking', 'expert_review','5');">
         Mio Fazzio Braking &amp; Safety
        </h3>
        <div class="acc-panel">
         <p>
          <span>
           The Yamaha Mio Fazzio boasts some of the best safety features to ensure the safety of the rider and the pillion in an accident.
          </span>
          <span>
           It incorporates full LED lights that enhance visibility on the road and offer a safe riding experience. This feature gives a modern look to the scooter. For added safety, it has power door locks and central locking. Mio Fizz also comes with various practical safety enhancements, like a pass switch that allows you to alert other motorists about your presence on the road. This proactive safety feature also provides alerts about any kind of engine issues to ensure a secure and safe riding experience and prevent breakdowns. The street riding mode allows you to optimize the performance of the scooter for congested or urban roads. All these features together contribute to a worry-free riding experience.
          </span>
         </p>
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="accordion border-top">
        <h3 class="acc-title scroll-to-parent-pos" onclick="gd.common.pushDataLayers('YamahaMio Fazzio.ModelPage.overviewTab', '', 'click_section', 'Widget_Tracking', 'expert_review','6');">
         Yamaha Mio Fazzio Verdict
        </h3>
        <div class="acc-panel">
         <p>
          <span>
           With the Yamaha Mio Fazzio, you can save on gas and cut your traveling time to half. It is easy to maneuver and has a very stylish and funky design that will appeal to even the most demanding customers. The lightweight dimensions of this scooter make it easy to park even on cramped streets. If you want a scooter with a retro-inspired design, tons of digital gadgets, and a striking silhouette, you can go to the Yamaha Mio Fazzio. It has everything that a good scooter should possess and rides like a dream on the road.
          </span>
         </p>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>

  <script>
   window.addEventListener('load', function() {
        const script = document.createElement('script');
        script.src = 'https://www.googletagservices.com/tag/js/gpt.js';
        document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild(script);
        document.querySelectorAll('.lazy-ad').forEach(element => {
            var refreshed = false;
            var threshold = 640;
            var scrollId = element.dataset.slot;
            if (element.offsetTop < threshold) {
                if (!refreshed) {
                    googletag.cmd.push(function () {
                        googletag.pubads().refresh([gptAdSlots[scrollId]]);
                    });
                    refreshed = true;
                }
            } else {
                var listener = function () {
                    var adSlotPos = element.offsetTop;
                    var adAlmostVisibleScrollValue = adSlotPos - 700;
                    if (window.scrollY >= adAlmostVisibleScrollValue && !refreshed) {
                        googletag.cmd.push(function () {
                            googletag.pubads().refresh([gptAdSlots[scrollId]]);
                        });
                        refreshed = true;
                        window.removeEventListener('scroll', listener);
                    }
                }
                window.addEventListener('scroll', listener);
            }
        })
    });
window.addEventListener('load', function() {
        setTimeout(function () {
            window.addEventListener('scroll', function() {
                showCookieConsentPopup();
            });
        }, 4000);
    });
  </script>

  <script>
   const userConsentInput = document.querySelector('input[name="RegisterForm[userConsent]"]');

    const fieldset = userConsentInput.closest('fieldset');
    const helpBlockDiv = fieldset.querySelector('.help-block');
    const labelElement = fieldset.querySelector('label');

    // Move the help-block div after the label for show error after input checkbox
    labelElement.insertAdjacentElement('afterend', helpBlockDiv);

    window.fbAsyncInit = function() {
        FB.init({
            //   appId      : '1397367364072943',
            appId: gd.config.facebookAppId,
            cookie: true,
            xfbml: true,
            version: 'v14.0'
        });

        FB.AppEvents.logPageView();

    };

    (function(d, s, id) {
        var js, fjs = d.getElementsByTagName(s)[0];
        if (d.getElementById(id)) {
            return;
        }
        js = d.createElement(s);
        js.id = id;
        js.src = "https://connect.facebook.net/en_US/sdk.js";
        fjs.parentNode.insertBefore(js, fjs);
    }(document, 'script', 'facebook-jssdk'));
  </script>
